### [311] [Credal Concept Bottleneck Models for Epistemic-Aleatoric Uncertainty Decomposition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24170)
*Tanmoy Mukherjee,Thomas Bailleux,Pierre Marquis,Zied Bouraoui*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: CREDENCE是一个概念瓶颈模型框架，通过将概念预测表示为概率区间（信域预测），分解认知不确定性和偶然不确定性，支持自动化、人工审查、数据收集等决策。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有概念瓶颈模型（CBM）输出点概率概念预测，混淆了认知不确定性（可减少的模型不确定）和偶然不确定性（不可减少的输入歧义），导致概念层面的不确定性难以解释和采取行动。

Method: CREDENCE将每个概念表示为信域预测（概率区间），通过多样化概念头之间的分歧推导认知不确定性，通过专用模糊度输出估计偶然不确定性（在有标注者分歧数据时进行对齐训练）。

Result: 认知不确定性与预测误差正相关，偶然不确定性与标注者分歧紧密相关，能提供超越误差相关性的决策指导。

Conclusion: CREDENCE通过分解两种不确定性，支持以下规定性决策：低不确定性自动化、高认知不确定性优先收集数据、高偶然不确定性路由至人工审查、两者都高时弃权。

Abstract: Concept Bottleneck Models (CBMs) predict through human-interpretable concepts, but they typically output point concept probabilities that conflate epistemic uncertainty (reducible model underspecification) with aleatoric uncertainty (irreducible input ambiguity). This makes concept-level uncertainty hard to interpret and, more importantly, hard to act upon. We introduce CREDENCE (Credal Ensemble Concept Estimation), a CBM framework that decomposes concept uncertainty by construction. CREDENCE represents each concept as a credal prediction (a probability interval), derives epistemic uncertainty from disagreement across diverse concept heads, and estimates aleatoric uncertainty via a dedicated ambiguity output trained to match annotator disagreement when available. The resulting signals support prescriptive decisions: automate low-uncertainty cases, prioritize data collection for high-epistemic cases, route high-aleatoric cases to human review, and abstain when both are high. Across several tasks, we show that epistemic uncertainty is positively associated with prediction errors, whereas aleatoric uncertainty closely tracks annotator disagreement, providing guidance beyond error correlation. Our implementation is available at the following link: https://github.com/Tankiit/Credal_Sets/tree/ensemble-credal-cbm

</details>


### [312] [Explanation Quality Assessment as Ranking with Listwise Rewards](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24176)
*Thomas Bailleux,Tanmoy Mukherjee,Emmanuel Lonca,Pierre Marquis,Zied Bouraoui*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出将解释质量评估重构为排序问题而非生成问题，通过训练奖励模型对多个候选解释进行排序，并发现排序损失优于回归、数据特征决定最优排序方法、数据质量比模型规模更重要，以及排序分数作为奖励能实现稳定收敛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统解释质量评估采用逐词生成最佳解释的方式，但这种方法存在分数压缩、难以区分不同质量等级的问题。作者希望将评估重构为排序问题，通过区分多个候选解释的相对质量来更有效地区分解释质量。

Method: 构建每个实例的多候选解释集，标注不同质量等级；训练列表式（ListNet）和逐对式（LambdaRank, RankNet）排序模型以保留序数结构；在多个领域测试排序损失与回归损失的对比效果；将排序分数用作策略优化的奖励信号。

Result: 排序损失在所有领域上一致优于回归损失；列表式目标在质量等级区分明显的场景表现最佳，逐对式方法对噪声标注更鲁棒；在精心策划的数据上，小型编码器模型可匹配大规模模型；排序奖励在回归奖励失败的场景中实现稳定收敛。

Conclusion: 解释质量评估应被视为排序问题而非生成问题；数据质量比模型规模更重要；排序损失的选择需根据数据特性决定；排序分数作为奖励信号在强化学习中具有显著优势。

Abstract: We reformulate explanation quality assessment as a ranking problem rather than a generation problem. Instead of optimizing models to produce a single "best" explanation token-by-token, we train reward models to discriminate among multiple candidate explanations and learn their relative quality. Concretely, we construct per-instance candidate sets with graded quality levels and train listwise and pairwise ranking models (ListNet, LambdaRank, RankNet) to preserve ordinal structure and avoid score compression typical of pointwise regression or binary preference objectives. We observe three findings: First, ranking losses consistently outperform regression on score separation across all domains tested. Second, the optimal ranking loss depends on data characteristics: listwise objectives excel with well-separated quality tiers, while pairwise methods are more robust to noisy natural annotations. Third, when trained on carefully curated and well-structured data, small encoder models can match models that are orders of magnitude larger, suggesting that data quality matters more than model scale. Finally, when used as rewards in policy optimization, ranking-based scores enable stable convergence in settings where regression-based rewards fail entirely. Code and data are available at: https://github.com/Tankiit/PPO_Learning_to_rank

</details>


### [313] [Adaptive ToR: Complexity-Aware Tree-Based Retrieval for Pareto-Optimal Multi-Intent NLU](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24219)
*Hee-Kyong Yoo,Wonbae Kim,Hyocheol Ahn*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出Adaptive Tree-of-Retrieval (Adaptive ToR)，一种复杂度感知的自适应检索架构，通过动态配置检索拓扑（单步快速路径或自适应深度层次路径）来平衡多意图自然语言理解中的准确率、延迟与计算效率。在NLU++基准上，相比固定深度基线，子集准确率提升9.7%达29.07%，延迟降低37.6%，LLM调用减少43.0%，Token消耗降低9.8%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法要么采用统一的单步检索（牺牲召回率），要么采用固定深度的层次分解（无论查询复杂度如何都引入过高延迟），缺乏根据查询复杂度动态调整检索策略的机制。

Method: 包含四个组件：(1) 查询树分类器：通过加权语言信号计算查询复杂度指数，将查询路由至单步路径或自适应深度层次路径；(2) 基于树的检索模块：递归将复杂查询分解为聚焦子查询；(3) 自适应剪枝模块：结合定量相似度门控与语义相关性评估的两阶段过滤，抑制指数级节点增长；(4) 检索重排序层：去重器优先管道+全局LLM重评分。

Result: NLU++基准（2,693个多意图查询）上：Subset Accuracy 29.07%，Micro-F1 71.79%，相对固定深度基线提升9.7%；延迟降低37.6%，LLM调用减少43.0%，Token消耗降低9.8%。26.92%查询通过单步路由在2.45秒内解决（d=0: Subset Accuracy 37.9%, Micro-F1 74.8%），Token消耗随深度增加4.9倍。

Conclusion: 验证了复杂度感知资源分配的有效性，在准确率、延迟和计算效率之间建立了帕累托最优平衡。

Abstract: Multi-intent natural language understanding requires retrieval systems that simultaneously achieve high accuracy and computational efficiency, yet existing approaches apply either uniform single-step retrieval that compromises recall or fixed-depth hierarchical decomposition that introduces excessive latency regardless of query complexity. This paper proposes Adaptive Tree-of-Retrieval (Adaptive ToR), a complexity-aware retrieval architecture that dynamically configures retrieval topology based on query characteristics. The system integrates four components: (1) a Query Tree Classifier computing a Query Complexity Index from weighted linguistic signals to route queries to either a rapid single-step path or an adaptive-depth hierarchical path; (2) a Tree-Based Retrieval module that recursively decomposes complex queries into focused sub-queries calibrated to predicted complexity; (3) an Adaptive Pruning Module employing two-stage filtering combining quantitative similarity gating with semantic relevance evaluation to suppress exponential node growth; and (4) a Retrieval Reranking Layer featuring a deduplicator-first pipeline and global LLM rescoring for production efficiency. Evaluation on the NLU++ benchmark (2,693 multi-intent queries across Banking and Hotel domains) yields 29.07% Subset Accuracy and 71.79% Micro-F1, a 9.7% relative improvement over fixed-depth baselines, while reducing latency by 37.6%, LLM invocations by 43.0%, and token consumption by 9.8%. Depth-wise analysis reveals that 26.92% of queries resolve within three seconds (2.45s mean latency) via single-step routing (d=0: 37.9% Subset Accuracy, 74.8% Micro-F1), while token consumption scales by 4.9x across depths, validating complexity-aware resource allocation and establishing Pareto-optimal balance across accuracy, latency, and computational efficiency.

To address this, we propose Alignment via VErified Self-correction DPO (AVES-DPO), a framework that aligns LVLMs using in-distribution data derived from the model's intrinsic knowledge. Our approach employs a consensus-based verification mechanism to diagnose diverse hallucinations and guides the model to self-correct, thereby generating preference pairs strictly compatible with its internal distribution. ### [315] [PhysNote: Self-Knowledge Notes for Evolvable Physical Reasoning in Vision-Language Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24443)
*Sinin Zhang,Yunfei Xie,Yuxuan Cheng,Haoyu Zhang,Tong Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出PhysNote框架，通过自生成的"知识笔记"外部化和精炼物理知识，解决VLM在动态真实场景中因时空身份漂移和推理洞察不稳定导致的物理推理失败问题，在PhysBench上达到56.68%准确率，比最佳多智能体基线提升4.96%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLM在教科书式物理问题上表现良好，但在需要时间一致性和跨帧因果推理的动态真实场景中频繁失败，根本原因在于(1)时空身份漂移：物体在连续帧中丢失物理身份，破坏因果链；(2)推理洞察的不稳定性：模型偶尔能给出正确推理但无法固化复用。

Method: PhysNote是一个智能体框架，包含三个核心机制：(1)时空规范化(stabilizes dynamic perception)稳定动态感知；(2)分层知识仓库(hierarchical knowledge repository)组织自生成洞察；(3)迭代推理循环(iterative reasoning loop)在视觉证据中验证假设并固化知识。

Result: 在PhysBench上，PhysNote达到56.68%整体准确率，比最佳多智能体基线提升4.96%，在全部四个物理推理领域均有一致性提升。

Conclusion: 外部化知识笔记机制能有效解决VLM在动态场景中的物理推理缺陷，通过将临时性推理结果固化为可复用的结构化知识，显著提升了模型在真实世界物理推理任务上的表现。

Abstract: Vision-Language Models (VLMs) have demonstrated strong performance on textbook-style physics problems, yet they frequently fail when confronted with dynamic real-world scenarios that require temporal consistency and causal reasoning across frames. We identify two fundamental challenges underlying these failures: (1) spatio-temporal identity drift, where objects lose their physical identity across successive frames and break causal chains, and (2) volatility of inference-time insights, where a model may occasionally produce correct physical reasoning but never consolidates it for future reuse. To address these challenges, we propose PhysNote, an agentic framework that enables VLMs to externalize and refine physical knowledge through self-generated "Knowledge Notes." PhysNote stabilizes dynamic perception through spatio-temporal canonicalization, organizes self-generated insights into a hierarchical knowledge repository, and drives an iterative reasoning loop that grounds hypotheses in visual evidence before consolidating verified knowledge. Experiments on PhysBench demonstrate that PhysNote achieves 56.68% overall accuracy, a 4.96% improvement over the best multi-agent baseline, with consistent gains across all four physical reasoning domains.

### [316] [Agentic clinical reasoning over longitudinal myeloma records: a retrospective evaluation against expert consensus](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24473)
*Johannes Moll,Jannik Lübberstedt,Christoph Nuernbergk,Jacob Stroh,Luisa Mertens,Anna Purcarea,Christopher Zirn,Zeineb Benchaaben,Fabian Drexel,Hartmut Häntze,Anirudh Narayanan,Friedrich Puttkammer,Andrei Zhukov,Jacqueline Lammert,Sebastian Ziegelmayer,Markus Graf,Marion Högner,Marcus Makowski,Florian Bassermann,Lisa C. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 回顾性评估811名骨髓瘤患者（2001-2026）的纵向临床记录（44,962份文档，1,334,677项实验室值），外部验证于MIMIC-IV。比较智能体推理系统与单次RAG、迭代RAG、全上下文输入在469对患者-问题（48个模板，三个复杂度级别）上的表现。参考标签由四位肿瘤科医生双重注释并由高级血液科医生裁定。

Result: 智能体系统达到79.6%一致性，超过迭代RAG（75.4%）和全上下文输入（75.8%）（p=0.006和0.007）。在复杂问题上提升+9.4pp（p=0.032），在最长记录上提升+13.5pp。系统错误率12.2%与专家分歧13.6%相当，但57.8%系统错误具有临床显著性，而专家仅18.8%。

Conclusion: 智能体推理是唯一超越共享上限的方法，优势集中在最复杂的问题和最长的记录上。但残余系统错误的临床后果更严重，需要在常规护理中进行前瞻性评估后才能将这些发现转化为患者获益。

Abstract: Multiple myeloma is managed through sequential lines of therapy over years to decades, with each decision depending on cumulative disease history distributed across dozens to hundreds of heterogeneous clinical documents. Whether LLM-based systems can synthesise this evidence at a level approaching expert agreement has not been established. A retrospective evaluation was conducted on longitudinal clinical records of 811 myeloma patients treated at a tertiary centre (2001-2026), covering 44,962 documents and 1,334,677 laboratory values, with external validation on MIMIC-IV. An agentic reasoning system was compared against single-pass retrieval-augmented generation (RAG), iterative RAG, and full-context input on 469 patient-question pairs from 48 templates at three complexity levels. Reference labels came from double annotation by four oncologists with senior haematologist adjudication. Iterative RAG and full-context input converged on a shared ceiling (75.4% vs 75.8%, p = 1.00). The agentic system reached 79.6% concordance (95% CI 76.4-82.8), exceeding both baselines (+3.8 and +4.2 pp; p = 0.006 and 0.007). Gains rose with question complexity, reaching +9.4 pp on criteria-based synthesis (p = 0.032), and with record length, reaching +13.5 pp in the top decile (n = 10). The system error rate (12.2%) was comparable to expert disagreement (13.6%), but severity was inverted: 57.8% of system errors were clinically significant versus 18.8% of expert disagreements. Agentic reasoning was the only approach to exceed the shared ceiling, with gains concentrated on the most complex questions and longest records. The greater clinical consequence of residual system errors indicates that prospective evaluation in routine care is required before these findings translate into patient benefit.

Method: 构建对齐多模态数据集LORE；采用分轨编码器-解码器架构，可基于任意观测模态子集进行条件生成，重建或预测基因组、转录组和蛋白质组中缺失的分子状态。

Result: 多模态条件显著提升序列重建质量；在RNA和蛋白质下游任务中取得SOTA性能；实现SOTA剪接预测并支持异构体感知推理；成功修复HBB剪接破坏突变而不还原原序列；针对PD-L1和hACE2结合位点设计出高置信度蛋白质序列；实现实验上下文建模的RNA化学探针测定预测。

Conclusion: MIMIC的对齐多模态生成建模为统一表征学习、条件预测和约束生物分子设计提供了强基础框架。

Abstract: Biological function emerges from coupled constraints across sequence, structure, regulation, evolution, and cellular context, yet most foundation models in biology are trained within one modality or for a fixed forward task. We present MIMIC, a generative multimodal foundation model trained on our newly curated and aligned dataset, LORE, linking nucleic acid, protein, evolutionary, structural, regulatory, and semantic/contextual modalities within partially observed biomolecular states. MIMIC uses a split-track encoder-decoder architecture to condition on arbitrary subsets of observed modalities and reconstruct or generate missing components of molecular state across the genome, transcriptome, and proteome. Multimodal conditioning consistently improves MIMIC's sequence reconstruction relative to sequence-only inputs, while its learned representations enable state-of-the-art performance on RNA and protein downstream tasks. MIMIC achieves state-of-the-art splicing prediction, and its joint generative formulation enables isoform-aware inference that further improves performance. Beyond prediction, the same generative framework supports constrained design. For RNA, MIMIC identifies corrective edits in a clinically relevant HBB splice-disrupting mutation without reverting it by using evolutionary and structural signals. For proteins, jointly conditioning on shape and surface chemistry of PD-L1 and hACE2 binding sites produces diverse, high-confidence sequences with strong in silico support for target binding. Finally, MIMIC uses experimental context as semantic conditioning to model assay-dependent RNA chemical probing, rather than treating context as a fixed output. Together, these results position MIMIC's aligned multimodal generative modeling as a strong foundation for unifying representation learning, conditional prediction, and constrained biomolecular design within a single model.

</details>

Interoception, conceived as the monitoring, integration, and regulation of internal signals, has proven relevant for understanding adaptive behavior in biological systems. The proposed framework organizes interoceptive contributions into three functional principles: homeostatic, allostatic, and enactive, each associated with distinct computational roles: internal viability regulation, anticipatory uncertainty-based re-evaluation, and active data generation through interaction. These principles are not intended as direct neurophysiological mappings, but as abstractions that inform the design of artificial agents with improved self-regulation and context-sensitive behavior. By embedding internal state variables and regulatory loops within these principles, AI systems can achieve more robust decision-making, calibrated uncertainty handling, and adaptive interaction strategies, particularly in uncertain and dynamic environments. This approach provides a concrete and testable pathway toward agents capable of functionally grounded self-regulation, with direct implications for human-computer interaction and assistive technologies. Ultimately, the interoceptive machine framework offers a unifying perspective on how internal-state regulation can enhance autonomy, adaptivity, and robustness in embodied AI systems

### [320] [Hierarchical Behaviour Spaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24558)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的层次化强化学习为每个选项使用单一奖励函数，限制了策略的表达能力。本文旨在通过允许控制器指定奖励函数的线性组合，扩展选项空间的表达能力，从而诱导更丰富的行为空间。

Method: 提出Hierarchical Behaviour Spaces (HBS)方法，核心创新在于用奖励函数的线性组合替代每个选项的单一奖励函数，让高层控制器可以灵活组合多个奖励信号来生成多样化的行为。

Result: 在NetHack Learning Environment上取得了强性能表现。通过系列实验发现，层次结构带来的性能提升主要源于增强了探索能力，而非传统认知中的长期推理能力。

Conclusion: HBS通过线性组合奖励函数扩展了选项空间的表达能力；层次结构在本文方法中的核心价值在于促进探索而非长期推理，这一发现与常规认知不同。

Abstract: Recent work in hierarchical reinforcement learning has shown success in scaling to billions of timesteps when learning over a set of predefined option reward functions. We show that, instead of using a single reward function per option, the reward functions can be effectively used to induce a space of behaviours, by letting the controller specify linear combinations over reward functions, allowing a more expressive set of policies to be represented. We call this method Hierarchical Behaviour Spaces (HBS). We evaluate HBS on the NetHack Learning Environment, demonstrating strong performance. We conduct a series of experiments and determine that, perhaps going against conventional wisdom, the benefits of hierarchy in our method come from increased exploration rather than long term reasoning.

However, without explicitly grounding and reasoning in structured traffic scenarios, LLMs often retrieve irrelevant provisions or miss applicable ones, yielding imprecise requirements. To address this, we propose a novel pipeline that grounds LLM reasoning in a traffic scenario taxonomy through node-wise anchors that encode hierarchical semantics. On Chinese traffic laws and OnSite dataset (5,897 scenarios), our method improves law-scenario matching by 29.1\% and increases the accuracy of derived mandatory and prohibitive requirements by 36.9\% and 38.2\%, respectively. ### [322] [FastOMOP: A Foundational Architecture for Reliable Agentic Real-World Evidence Generation on OMOP CDM data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24572)
*Niko Moeller-Grell,Shihao Shenzhang,Zhangshu Joshua Jiang,Richard JB Dobson,Vishnu V Chandrabalan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: FastOMOP 是一个开源的多智能体架构，通过分离治理、可观测性和编排三个基础设施层，实现了对 OMOP CDM 数据中真实世界证据生成的灵活、安全且可审计的自动化。该系统采用过程边界治理，通过确定性验证确保即使智能体被攻破或产生幻觉也无法绕过安全控制，在三个数据集上取得了 0.84-0.94 的可靠性评分和完美的对抗性/越界拦截率，证明 RWE 部署的可靠性瓶颈在于架构而非模型能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 OMOP CDM 数据生成 RWE 的过程仍依赖手动操作，需要临床、流行病学和技术专家共同参与。LLM 和多智能体系统虽在临床任务中展现出潜力，但智能体系统固有的涌现行为、协调失败和安全风险缺乏有效的治理机制，目前没有基础设施能够确保智能体化的 RWE 生成在全生命周期中保持灵活、安全和可审计。

Method: FastOMOP 采用三层分离架构：治理层在过程边界通过确定性验证强制执行安全约束，独立于智能体推理过程；可观测性层提供全生命周期审计追踪；编排层协调可插拔的智能体团队（包括表型分析、研究设计和统计分析团队）。治理机制确保即使智能体被攻破或产生幻觉，也无法绕过过程边界的确定性安全控制，智能体团队通过受控的工具暴露继承这些安全保证。

Result: 在 Synthea 合成数据、MIMIC-IV 和兰开夏教学医院 NHS 真实数据集（IDRIL）上，使用自然语言到 SQL 的智能体团队进行验证。FastOMOP 取得了 0.84-0.94 的可靠性评分，对抗性攻击和越界请求的拦截率达到完美水平（100%），证明过程边界治理能够在独立于模型选择的情况下提供安全保证。

Conclusion: RWE 部署中的可靠性差距本质上是架构问题而非模型能力问题。FastOMOP 作为一种有治理架构的方案，为渐进式自动化 RWE 生成建立了基础，其过程边界治理机制确保了安全性与模型无关，为未来更广泛的临床证据自动化生成提供了可行的架构范式。

Abstract: The Observational Medical Outcomes Partnership Common Data Model (OMOP CDM), maintained by the Observational Health Data Sciences and Informatics (OHDSI) collaboration, enabled the harmonisation of electronic health records data of nearly one billion patients in 83 countries. Yet generating real-world evidence (RWE) from these repositories remains a manual process requiring clinical, epidemiological and technical expertise. LLMs and multi-agent systems have shown promise for clinical tasks, but RWE automation exposes a fundamental challenge: agentic systems introduce emergent behaviours, coordination failures and safety risks that existing approaches fail to govern. No infrastructure exists to ensure agentic RWE generation is flexible, safe and auditable across the lifecycle. We introduce FastOMOP, an open-source multi-agent architecture that addresses this gap by separating three infrastructure layers, governance, observability and orchestration, from pluggable agent-teams. Governance is enforced at the process boundary through deterministic validation independent of agent reasoning, ensuring no compromised or hallucinating agent can bypass safety controls. Agent teams for phenotyping, study design and statistical analysis inherit these guarantees through controlled tool exposure. We validated FastOMOP using a natural-language-to-SQL agent team across three OMOP CDM datasets: synthetic data from Synthea, MIMIC-IV and a real-world NHS dataset from Lancashire Teaching Hospitals (IDRIL). FastOMOP achieved reliability scores of 0.84-0.94 with perfect adversarial and out-of-scope block rates, demonstrating process-boundary governance delivers safety guarantees independent of model choice. These results indicate that the reliability gap in RWE deployment is architectural rather than model capability, and establish FastOMOP as a governed architecture for progressive RWE automation.

Abstract: Vision-language models (VLMs) are increasingly proposed as general-purpose tools for scientific data interpretation, yet their reliability on real astronomical observations across diverse modalities remains untested. We present AstroVLBench, a comprehensive benchmark comprising over 4,100 expert-verified instances across five tasks spanning optical imaging, radio interferometry, multi-wavelength photometry, time-domain light curves, and optical spectroscopy. Evaluating six frontier models, we find that performance is strongly modality-dependent: while one model (Gemini 3 Pro) emerges as the most consistently capable across tasks, task-specific strengths vary, and all models substantially underperform domain-specialized methods. Mechanistic ablations reveal that performance depends not only on directing attention to salient visual features but also on grounding those features in physical knowledge. Phenomenological prompts describing what to look for improve accuracy by sharpening model focus, but physical prompts explaining why those features matter perform better overall and yield more balanced classifications with reduced class-specific bias. Consistent with this picture, presenting the underlying one-dimensional measurements directly as numerical tables instead of rendered plots yields up to 13 percentage points improvement. Reasoning quality analysis further demonstrates that, without explicit physical grounding, models may reach correct predictions from phenomenologically plausible cues while providing physically imprecise justifications, establishing that accuracy alone is insufficient for trustworthy scientific deployment. These findings provide the first systematic, multi-modal baselines for VLMs in observational astronomy and identify the specific representation, grounding, and reasoning bottlenecks where current models fail.

### [324] [XGRAG: A Graph-Native Framework for Explaining KG-based Retrieval-Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24623)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出XGRAG框架，采用基于图的扰动策略，量化单个图组件（如节点、边）对模型答案的因果贡献，生成因果层面的解释。

Result: 在NarrativeQA、FairyTaleQA、TriviaQA上，XGRAG相比RAG-Ex在F1分数上提升14.81%；解释与图中心性度量高度相关，验证了其捕获图结构的能力。

However, GraphRAG reasoning process remains a black-box, limiting our ability to understand how specific pieces of structured knowledge influence the final output. Existing explainability (XAI) methods for RAG systems, designed for text-based retrieval, are limited to interpreting an LLM response through the relational structures among knowledge components, creating a critical gap in transparency and trustworthiness. To address this, we introduce XGRAG, a novel framework that generates causally grounded explanations for GraphRAG systems by employing graph-based perturbation strategies, to quantify the contribution of individual graph components on the model answer. We conduct extensive experiments comparing XGRAG against RAG-Ex, an XAI baseline for standard RAG, and evaluate its robustness across various question types, narrative structures and LLMs. Our results demonstrate a 14.81% improvement in explanation quality over the baseline RAG-Ex across NarrativeQA, FairyTaleQA, and TriviaQA, evaluated by F1-score measuring alignment between generated explanations and original answers. Furthermore, XGRAG explanations exhibit a strong correlation with graph centrality measures, validating its ability to capture graph structure. XGRAG provides a scalable and generalizable approach towards trustworthy AI through transparent, graph-based explanations that enhance the interpretability of RAG systems.

### [325] [The Price of Agreement: Measuring LLM Sycophancy in Agentic Financial Applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24668)
*Zhenyu Zhao,Aparna Balagopalan,Adi Agrawal,Dilshoda Yergasheva,Waseem Alshikh,Daniel M. Bikel*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文评估了LLM在金融智能体任务中的谄媚行为（sycophancy），即模型倾向于认同用户表达的观点而非坚持正确性。研究发现：1）面对用户反驳或矛盾时，模型性能仅出现低至中等下降，与先前的通用领域发现不同；2）存在用户偏好信息与参考答案相矛盾时，大多数模型会失败；3）基准测试了基于预训练LLM的输入过滤等多种恢复模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着LLM在金融系统中的广泛应用，评估其安全性和鲁棒性变得至关重要。LLM在通用领域中常表现出谄媚行为（优先同意用户表达的观点而非正确性），但该现象在金融智能体任务中尚未被充分研究。

Method: 设计了一套金融智能体任务套件，通过引入用户反驳/矛盾（与参考答案冲突）以及用户偏好信息（与参考答案相矛盾）来测试LLM的谄媚行为，并基准测试了基于预训练LLM的输入过滤等恢复策略。

Result: 1) 面对用户反驳时，模型性能仅出现低至中等程度的下降，这与通用领域中的谄媚现象程度不同；2) 当用户偏好信息与参考答案矛盾时，大多数模型会失败；3) 预训练LLM输入过滤等恢复模式被用于基准测试。

Conclusion: 金融智能体任务中的谄媚行为与通用领域存在差异，尤其在面对用户反驳时影响较小，但用户偏好信息的矛盾输入仍会导致多数模型失败，需要有效的恢复机制。

Abstract: Given the increased use of LLMs in financial systems today, it becomes important to evaluate the safety and robustness of such systems. One failure mode that LLMs frequently display in general domain settings is that of sycophancy. That is, models prioritize agreement with expressed user beliefs over correctness, leading to decreased accuracy and trust. In this work, we focus on evaluating sycophancy that LLMs display in agentic financial tasks. Our findings are three-fold: first, we find the models show only low to modest drops in performance in the face of user rebuttals or contradictions to the reference answer, which distinguishes sycophancy that models display in financial agentic settings from findings in prior work. Second, we introduce a suite of tasks to test for sycophancy by user preference information that contradicts the reference answer and find that most models fail in the presence of such inputs. Lastly, we benchmark different modes of recovery such as input filtering with a pretrained LLM.

</details>


### [326] [Governing What You Cannot Observe: Adaptive Runtime Governance for Autonomous AI Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24686)
*German Marin,Jatin Chaudhary*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出信息可行性原则和Agent可行性框架，通过统计估计器（KL散度、z检验、序列匹配）和标量生存指数VI(t)实现AI Agent的预测性治理，在不修改代码的情况下检测行为漂移和对抗适应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自主AI Agent即使保持完全授权，也可能因行为漂移、对手适应和决策模式变化而变得不安全，且无需任何代码变更。现有方法缺乏形式化的理论保障来应对这类动态风险。

Method: 基于Aubin的生存理论，提出Agent可行性框架，包含三个必要条件（监测P1、预测P2、单调限制P3）；实例化为RiskGate系统，使用KL散度估计未观测风险、分段对比z检验检测统计漂移、序列模式匹配追踪行为轨迹，并实现闭环自动驾驶仪（kill-switch作为最后手段）和标量生存指数VI(t)∈[-1,+1]及一阶t*预测。

Result: 提供了理论框架、参考实现RiskGate，以及针对已发表的Agent失败分类法的分析覆盖度；定量实证评估作为后续工作。

Conclusion: 三个属性（监测、预测、单调限制）对已记录的失败模式是各自必要且共同充分的；信息可行性原则将治理问题简化为估计未观测风险上界与行动容量之间的安全裕度比较。

Abstract: Autonomous AI agents can remain fully authorized and still become unsafe as behavior drifts, adversaries adapt, and decision patterns shift without any code change. We propose the \textbf{Informational Viability Principle}: governing an agent reduces to estimating a bound on unobserved risk $\hat{B}(x) = U(x) + SB(x) + RG(x)$ and allowing an action only when its capacity $S(x)$ exceeds $\hat{B}(x)$ by a safety margin. The \textbf{Agent Viability Framework}, grounded in Aubin's viability theory, establishes three properties -- monitoring (P1), anticipation (P2), and monotonic restriction (P3) -- as individually necessary and collectively sufficient for documented failure modes. \textbf{RiskGate} instantiates the framework with dedicated statistical estimators (KL divergence, segment-vs-rest $z$-tests, sequential pattern matching), a fail-secure monotonic pipeline, and a closed-loop Autopilot formalised as an instance of Aubin's regulation map with kill-switch-as-last-resort; a scalar Viability Index $VI(t) \in [-1,+1]$ with first-order $t^*$ prediction transforms governance from reactive to predictive. Contributions are the theoretical framework, the reference implementation, and analytical coverage against published agent-failure taxonomies; quantitative empirical evaluation is scoped as follow-up work.

</details>

### [327] [The Elusive Nature of Roughness: Linking Hydraulics and Graph Theory for Water Distribution Networks Model Calibration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22809)
*Karol Dykiert,Mateusz Stolarski,Michał Czuba,Wojciech Cieżak,Piotr Bródka*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了如何通过管网分区（利用水力与图论属性）提高大规模配水管网中管道粗糙度校准的效率与可靠性。实验表明，基于属性分组的方法（特别是结合图论数据）能产生稳定、可重复的结果，密度聚类在特定配置下可降低计算成本。该方法为传统人工启发式方法提供了一种系统、可复现且计算高效的替代方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模配水管网中管道粗糙度的准确估计常受限于传统现场方法的高成本，亟需一种系统化、低成本且可重复的参数校准方法。

Method: 以真实管网的高保真模型为基准，对比了密度聚类（DBSCAN）与基于拓扑的（如k-means）分组策略的优化校准效果，评估了水力属性与图论属性对分组质量的影响。

Result: 属性分组方法在校准水力意义重大的管道时能获得与人工校准相当的稳定可重复结果；加入图论数据可提高校准鲁棒性；密度聚类在某些配置下能达到与k-means相近的精度并降低计算量。

Conclusion: 拓扑信息驱动的分组策略为传统人工启发式方法提供了一种系统、可复现且计算高效的替代方案，管网结构在可靠参数估计中扮演关键角色，但该方法并未消除所有不确定性来源。

Abstract: Accurate pipe roughness estimation in large-scale water distribution networks is often hindered by the high cost of traditional field methods. This study investigates whether network partitioning, by utilizing hydraulic and graph-derived attributes, can enhance the calibration of these parameters. Using a high-fidelity model of a real network as a benchmark, we evaluate density-based clustering, and topology-driven grouping strategies. Optimization experiments demonstrate that attribute-based grouping yields stable, repeatable results comparable to manual calibration for hydraulically significant pipes. While hydraulic attributes generate more distinct cluster structures, the inclusion of graph-based data improves calibration robustness by stabilizing the optimization process. Notably, density-based clustering achieves similar accuracy to k-means while reducing computational effort in specific configurations. Although the method does not eliminate all sources of uncertainty, results suggest that topology-informed grouping provides a systematic, reproducible, and computationally efficient alternative to manual heuristics, highlighting the critical role of network structure in reliable parameter estimation.

### [328] [Learning to Trust AI and Data-driven models in Data Assimilation through a Multifidelity Ensemble Gaussian Mixture Filter Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23060)
*Andrey A. Popov*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合理论驱动（可信）与数据驱动（不可信但快速）模型的多保真集成高斯混合滤波器（MF-EnGMF），通过核密度估计中的带宽缩放因子作为信任度量，并利用期望最大化方法自适应计算信任值，实现了在高维数据同化中利用少量理论驱动样本进行收敛推断，有效抑制了数据驱动模型的幻觉问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数据驱动（AI）模型虽然快速准确，但容易产生虚假、非物理的"幻觉"结果，被视为不可信方法；而理论驱动方法虽慢但物理真实可信。两者各有优劣，需结合以建立可量化的信任机制。

Method: 提出多保真集成高斯混合滤波器（MF-EnGMF）及其自适应信任版本。利用核密度估计中的带宽缩放因子表示对理论驱动和数据驱动模型的信任度；通过期望最大化（EM）方法自适应计算信任度量；将两者融合为粒子滤波器，实现高维数据同化。

Result: 在静态香蕉问题及Lorenz '96方程的序贯滤波示例上验证，表明该方法能够在欠采样区域（理论驱动样本数低于系统维度）实现高维收敛推断。

Conclusion: 通过理论驱动与数据驱动方法的协同使用，可以建立相对信任度量，构建可信赖的混合方法论，有效解决数据驱动模型在高维数据同化中的幻觉问题。

Abstract: AI and data-driven models have large potential for data assimilation applications by creating fast and accurate forecasts. Their tendency to produce spurious inaccurate, nonphysical results -- hallucination -- however, raises a serious question about their long-term use, and can be categorized as untrustworthy methods. Theory-driven methods on the other hand are slow, but are capable of staying physically realistic due to their mathematical underpinning, and can be categorized as trustworthy methods. We argue that by making use of these methods in tandem, it is possible to build a relative measure of trust between the theory-driven and data-driven methods that results in a combined trustworthy methodology. We argue, and then show, that the bandwidth scaling factors in the kernel density estimates can be used to represent our trust in the theory-driven and data-driven models. We provide for ways in which these measures of trust can be adaptively computed through an expectation-maximization approach. We combine all of these ideas to create the multifidelity ensemble Gaussian mixture filter and its adaptive trust version, which are particle filters capable of high-dimensional data assimilation. We validate our ideas on both a static banana problem and on a sequential filtering example with the Lorenz '96 equations, showing that it is possible to create a particle filter that is capable of high dimensional convergent inference in the undersampled regime -- when the number of theory-driven samples is less than the dimension of the system.

</details>


### [329] [In-context modeling as a retrain-free paradigm for foundation models in computational science](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23098)
*Lingfeng Li,Zhuoyuan Li,Shun Li,Kaixin Zhan,Huajian Gao,Changqing Chen,Liu Yang*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文提出上下文建模（ICM）范式，无需重新训练即可从观测场直接推断物理关系。该模型以物理信息方式、无监督地利用控制方程训练，单一模型可泛化至未见材料、几何与加载条件。在超弹性材料上验证，与有限元仿真集成，并表现出类似基础模型的可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 构建能够跨物理系统泛化而无需重新训练的模型是计算科学的核心挑战。

Method: 提出In-Context Modeling (ICM)范式，将测量数据作为物理上下文，通过单次前向传播进行推理；采用物理信息、无标签的方式，利用控制方程进行训练。

Result: 单一模型在超弹性材料上泛化至未见材料、几何与加载条件；与有限元仿真集成并通过实验全场测量验证；性能随数据多样性和计算预算增加而提升，展现出有利的缩放行为。

Conclusion: 将物理建模重新定义为上下文推理，建立了无需重新训练的可迁移科学学习范式，为计算科学中的可扩展建模奠定基础。

Abstract: Building models that generalize across physical systems without retraining remains a central challenge in computational science. Here we introduce In-Context Modeling (ICM), a retrain-free paradigm that infers physical relationships directly from observational fields. Rather than encoding system-specific behavior in fixed parameters, ICM assimilates measurements as physical context and performs inference through a single forward pass. Trained in a physics-informed, label-free manner using governing equations, a single model generalizes across unseen materials, geometries, and loading conditions. Demonstrated on hyperelasticity, ICM integrates with finite-element simulations and is validated using experimental full-field measurements. Moreover, performance improves with increasing data diversity and computational budget, exhibiting favorable scaling behavior analogous to foundation models. By recasting physical modeling as in-context inference, this work establishes a transferable paradigm for retrain-free scientific learning and a foundation for scalable modeling across computational science.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Recent years have seen growing application potential for Lattice-skin Plate Structures in advanced manufacturing fields such as aerospace and automotive engineering. For multiscale performance evaluation of such structures, conventional homogenization methods for lattice-filled volume structures are often used for equivalent analysis. However, in finite-thickness Lattice-skin Plate Structures, periodic boundary conditions imposed along the three orthogonal directions of the representative cell cannot adequately capture the boundary effect of the free surfaces in the thickness direction, which introduces bias into the prediction of effective properties. To reduce this bias, this study develops and open-sources a homogenization method for Lattice-skin Plate Structures, forming an open-source computational framework for this class of structures. Representative numerical examples show that the framework can stably extract effective plate/shell stiffness matrices and can be extended to predict multiphase material properties and analyze steady-state heat conduction. ### [331] [Partition-of-Unity Gaussian Kolmogorov-Arnold Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23599)
*Amir Nooeizadegan*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文提出分区归一化高斯KAN（PU-GKAN），通过Shepard型归一化将高斯基函数值除以其局部中心之和，实现精确常数复现和有限特征核解释。实验表明该方法降低了对尺度参数ε的敏感性，提升了验证精度和训练稳定性，在多种任务中表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高斯基函数在KAN中提供了高效灵活的替代方案，但标准高斯KAN对尺度参数ε敏感，训练不稳定。作者希望通过分区归一化（partition-of-unity）机制来稳定RBF基KAN的训练过程，降低对超参数ε的敏感性。

Method: 提出PU-GKAN，采用Shepard型归一化：每个边上高斯基函数值除以其固定中心上的局部和，产生分区归一化特征映射。从有限特征和加性核视角统一了标准GKAN和PU-GKAN的表述，明确了层核和特征矩阵。为ε设计了实用尺度选择区间，下界由相邻中心重叠决定，上界由保守的条件数阈值决定。

Result: PU-GKAN降低了对ε的敏感性，对大多数光滑和中等非光滑目标提升了验证精度，训练行为更稳定。优势在样本量和中心数扫描、高维架构、Matérn RBF基以及Helmholtz和波动方程的物理信息示例中均保持一致。

Conclusion: Shepard型分区归一化是一种简单有效的RBF基KAN稳定机制，PU-GKAN在保持标准KAN结构的同时显著提升了训练稳定性和泛化性能。

Abstract: Gaussian basis functions provide an efficient and flexible alternative to spline activations in KANs. In this work, we introduce the partition-of-unity Gaussian KAN (PU-GKAN), a Shepard-type normalized Gaussian KAN in which the Gaussian basis values on each edge are divided by their local sum over fixed centers. This produces a partition-of-unity feature map with trainable coefficients, while preserving the standard edge-based KAN structure. The normalized construction gives exact constant reproduction at the edge level and admits an explicit finite-feature kernel interpretation.
  We formulate both the standard Gaussian KAN (GKAN) and PU-GKAN from a finite-feature and additive-kernel viewpoint, making the induced layer kernels and empirical feature matrices explicit. Using the first-layer feature matrix as the reference object, we adopt a practical scale-selection interval for \(ε\), with the lower endpoint determined by adjacent-center overlap and the upper endpoint determined by a conservative conditioning threshold. Numerical experiments show that PU-GKAN reduces sensitivity to \(ε\), improves validation accuracy for most smooth and moderately non-smooth targets, and gives more stable training behavior. The benefit persists across sample-size and center-number sweeps, higher-dimensional architectures, Matérn RBF bases, and physics-informed examples involving Helmholtz and wave equations. These results indicate that Shepard-type partition-of-unity normalization is a simple and effective stabilization mechanism for RBF-based KANs.

</details>

Traffic is synthesised from volumes, composition, and vehicle dynamics, with vehicles represented as 3D systems. Vehicle-pavement interaction adopts ISO roughness with transverse coherence, and wind turbulence follows the Kármán spectrum with Davenport coherence. The framework enables accurate performance assessment and informs serviceability criteria and design optimisation for long-span bridges.

### [333] [Comparative Evaluation of Modern Deep Learning Methodologies for Portfolio Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24486)
*Samuel Ozechi,Banjo Francis,Wisdom Yakanu,Joe Wayne Byers*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本研究提出一个融合深度学习架构与传统金融模型的组合优化框架，在2015-2023年跨资产数据上评估了GNN、DRL、Transformer和Autoencoder等模型的表现。结果表明混合模型（如Transformer+GNN）在稳定性和风险控制上表现最优，而结合良好校准输入的MVO取得了最高累积回报和夏普比率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 使用2015-2023年股票、ETF和债券的历史数据，分别评估GNN、DRL、Transformer、Autoencoder四种深度学习模型，以及Transformer+GNN和Autoencoder+DRL两种混合架构。通过回测，使用波动率、累积收益、最大回撤、年化收益和夏普比率等指标，对比等权重、60/40配置和MVO等七种策略。

Result: Transformer+GNN混合模型实现了最低的波动率和最大回撤；MVO结合良好校准输入时取得最高累积回报和夏普比率；单独DRL因结构感知不足表现欠佳；Autoencoder行为类似等权重策略；混合模型在稳定性和风险控制方面表现优越。

Abstract: This study proposes a portfolio optimization framework that integrates advanced deep learning architectures with traditional financial models to enhance risk-adjusted performance. The models jointly address covariance estimation, return forecasting, dynamic asset allocation, and dimensionality reduction. Hybrid approaches such as Transformer+GNN and Autoencoder+DRL are also explored to capture both relational and temporal market structures. Performance is assessed through backtesting using metrics including volatility, cumulative return, maximum drawdown, annualized return, and Sharpe ratio across seven strategies, including Equal-Weighted, 60/40 allocation, and Mean-Variance Optimization (MVO). Results show that hybrid models provide superior stability and risk control, with Transformer+GNN achieving the lowest volatility and drawdown. MVO, when paired with well-calibrated inputs, delivers the highest cumulative return and Sharpe ratio, highlighting the continued relevance of traditional methods. Standalone DRL underperforms due to limited structural awareness, while Autoencoders exhibit behavior similar to Equal-Weight strategies, emphasizing the need for dynamic policy learning. These findings align with existing literature on relational modeling and feature compression in finance. Overall, the study demonstrates that combining deep learning with financial theory yields robust and adaptive portfolio strategies and suggests exploring latent representations within traditional optimization frameworks to improve scalability and performance.

### [334] [VEHRON: A Configuration-Driven BEV Simulation Framework for Subsystem-Level Studies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24726)

Main category: cs.CE

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 早期纯电动汽车研究中的分析工作流常分散在电子表格、笔记本和项目脚本中，导致复用、审计和扩展困难，亟需一个统一的、可追溯的标准化仿真框架。

Method: 基于Python构建，采用YAML配置、小型仿真引擎、共享状态总线、模型注册表、基于Schema的配置加载，支持外部Python文件加载自定义电池和HVAC模型，以命令行方式执行纵向仿真并输出案例包。

Result: 实现了一个可运行的命令行工作流，将车辆定义与测试用例定义组合执行仿真，生成时间序列、案例包（含输入、配置、元数据及标准图表），支持低阶电池、热管理、辅助负载和HVAC模型。

Conclusion: VEHRON为纯电动汽车纵向仿真提供了结构清晰、可审计、可扩展的开源解决方案，目前专注于低速纵向仿真，存在当前模型精度和覆盖范围的限制，未来可进一步扩展。

Abstract: In practical early-stage battery-electric vehicle studies, analysis workflows may become fragmented across spreadsheets, notebooks, and project-specific scripts, making reuse, audit, and extension harder. VEHRON is an open-source Python framework for a deterministic, traceable workflow built around prescribed-speed longitudinal simulation of battery-electric vehicles using validated YAML configuration, packaged drive-cycle resources, interchangeable subsystem models, and auditable case outputs. VEHRON currently runs as a command-line workflow in which a vehicle definition and a testcase definition are combined to execute a simulation, emit a flat time series, and write a case package containing copied inputs, resolved configuration, summary metadata, and standard plots. Architecturally, VEHRON is organized around a small simulation engine, a shared state bus, a registry of model selections, schema-based configuration loading, and extension points for custom battery and HVAC models loaded from external Python files. VEHRON currently focuses on battery-electric longitudinal simulation with low-order battery, thermal, auxiliary-load, and HVAC models. This paper explains how VEHRON is structured, how it is used, which models it implements, and where its present limits lie. Source code is available at https://github.com/vehron-dev/vehron, with archived release metadata recorded under DOI https://doi.org/10.5281/zenodo.19820111.

</details>

### [335] [Distance Field Rasterization for End-to-End Mesh Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23537)
*Jinkai Cui,Kaiwen Song,Chumeng Niu,Juyong Zhang*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: 本文提出SDFRaster，一种可光栅化的有符号距离场(SDF)表示方法，通过结合光栅化效率与SDF的显式表面表征，在四面体网格上优化连续SDF并集成可微行进四面体，实现无需后处理的端到端网格重建，在DTU和Tanks and Temples上取得了更高质量和更完整的表面重建，同时存储成本更低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于光栅化的方法虽能实现实时新视角合成，但其体素基元无法直接提供全局一致的表面表示，表面提取依赖启发式后处理；而隐式SDF方法能提供明确定义的表面，但通常需要计算昂贵的射线步进。两类方法之间存在效率与表面质量的鸿沟。

Method: 从Delaunay四面体化出发，在四面体网格上优化连续SDF，通过光栅化四面体并对其贡献进行alpha合成来实现高效渲染；同时将可微行进四面体(Differentiable Marching Tetrahedra)集成到优化循环中，实现无需后处理网格提取的端到端网格重建。

Result: 在DTU和Tanks and Temples数据集上的实验表明，SDFRaster相比现有最先进方法，实现了更高质量、更完整的表面重建，且存储成本更低。

Conclusion: SDFRaster成功弥合了光栅化效率与SDF显式表面表征之间的差距，为实时高质量三维重建提供了一种新的有效范式。

Abstract: Rasterization based methods have recently enabled high-quality novel view synthesis at real-time rates, but their underlying volumetric primitives do not expose a direct, globally consistent surface representation, leaving sur face extraction to heuristic post-processing. In contrast, implicit signed dis tance field (SDF) methods provide well-defined surfaces but are typically optimized with computationally expensive ray marching. We propose SD FRaster, a rasterizable SDF representation that bridges this gap by combin ing the efficiency of rasterization with signed distance field for end-to-end mesh reconstruction. Starting from a Delaunay tetrahedralization, we op timize a continuous SDF over a tetrahedral grid and render it efficiently by rasterizing tetrahedra and alpha-compositing their contributions. We further integrate differentiable Marching Tetrahedra into the optimization loop, enablingend-to-endmeshreconstructionwithoutpost-processingmesh extraction. Experiments on DTU and Tanks and Temples demonstrate that SDFRaster achieves higher-quality and more complete surface reconstruc tions with lower storage cost than state-of-the-art approaches. Project page: https://ustc3dv.github.io/SDFRaster/

</details>


### [336] [Progressive-Iterative Fairing of Curves and Surfaces with Localized Control Point Adjustment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23590)
*Jia Lin,Hongwei Lin,Weixian Huang,Azan Zhang*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于控制点调整的渐进迭代光顺方法，通过为每个控制点分配独立权重实现局部和全局形状光顺，并提供了自动控制点选择方法，消除了对人工交互的依赖。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统曲线曲面光顺方法通常应用全局修改，缺乏细粒度控制能力，且依赖人工交互。

Method: 提出渐进迭代光顺方法，为每个控制点分配独立权重，实现精确的局部形状调整；同时提供自动控制点选择方法。

Result: 数值实验证明了该方法的效率和有效性。

Conclusion: 该方法兼具全局和局部光顺能力，消除了对人工交互的依赖，实现了精细化的形状控制。

Abstract: Curve and surface fairing is crucial in computer-aided geometric design, influencing product quality, physical performance, and aesthetics. Traditional methods often apply global modifications, lacking fine-grained control. This paper introduces a novel progressive-iterative fairing method based on control point adjustment. By assigning independent weights to each control point, our approach enables precise, localized shape adjustments. The method functions both globally and locally, allowing for comprehensive shape fairing and fine control over the fairing effect. Furthermore, this paper provides an automatic control point selection method to adjust shapes, thereby eliminating the reliance on manual interaction. Numerical experiments demonstrate the efficiency and effectiveness of our approach.

### [337] [From Visual Synthesis to Interactive Worlds: Toward Production-Ready 3D Asset Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23629)
*Jiafeng Wu,Zhuofan Lou,Jian Liu,Dazhao Du,Chunchao Guo,Song Guo*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: 本文系统综述了面向交互式环境的3D内容生成技术，围绕资产生产管线（而非算法类别）构建二维分类法：横向区分通用物体、角色和场景三类资产，纵向覆盖从数据基础、几何合成到拓扑优化、UV展开、PBR材质、骨骼绑定和场景装配的完整生产生命周期，评估了当前方法在几何保真度、外观质量、资产可用性和场景级物理合理性方面的表现，并指出了数据质量、生成可控性、端到端资产化和物理接地生成等开放挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管3D生成建模技术快速进步，但其输出与交互式应用（游戏开发、具身AI、世界模拟、数字孪生、空间计算）所要求的工业级标准之间存在持续差距——引擎级约束涉及拓扑、UV参数化、基于物理的材质、骨骼绑定和物理感知场景布局，而现有方法多孤立地生成视觉上合理的形状，未考虑下游部署的工程需求。

Method: 采用二维分类法组织文献：横轴按资产层级（通用物体、角色、场景）划分；纵轴按生产管线生命周期（数据基础→几何合成→拓扑优化→UV展开→PBR外观→骨骼绑定→场景装配）追踪，同时整合了涵盖几何保真度、外观质量、资产可用性和场景级物理合理性的评估指标与协议。

Result: 系统评估了当前各方法在各管线阶段的生成能力及其输出是否可直接用于下游引擎和仿真平台，揭示了从"生成视觉合理形状"到"生成可直接部署资产"之间的系统性差距。

Conclusion: 生产就绪型3D内容是新兴交互式世界模型和具身智能系统的基础设施，当前核心挑战在于数据质量、生成可控性、端到端资产化（即从生成到可部署资产的完整自动化）以及物理接地生成。

Abstract: Three-dimensional content generation has progressed from producing isolated, visually plausible shapes to constructing structured assets that can be deployed in real-time interactive environments. This trajectory is driven by converging demands from game development, embodied AI, world simulation, digital twins, and spatial computing, all of which require 3D content that goes beyond surface appearance to satisfy engine-level constraints on topology, UV parameterization, physically based materials, skeletal rigging, and physics-aware scene layout. Despite rapid advances in generative modeling, a persistent gap separates the outputs of current methods from the production-ready standard expected by interactive applications. This survey addresses that gap by organizing the literature around the asset production pipeline rather than algorithmic families. Along the horizontal axis we distinguish three asset tiers, namely general objects, characters, and scenes, while the vertical axis traces each tier through the full production lifecycle from data foundations and geometry synthesis through topology optimization, UV unwrapping, PBR appearance, rigging, and scene assembly. Through this two-dimensional taxonomy we assess not only what current methods can generate but whether their outputs are directly usable in downstream engines and simulation platforms. We further consolidate evaluation metrics and protocols that span geometric fidelity, appearance quality, asset usability, and scene-level physical plausibility. The survey concludes by identifying open challenges in data quality, generation controllability, end-to-end assetization, and physically grounded generation, and by situating production-ready 3D content as foundational infrastructure for emerging interactive world models and embodied intelligent systems.

### [338] [Personalizing Causal Audio-Driven Facial Motion via Dynamic Multi-modal Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23692)
*Xuangeng Chu,Yu Han,Wei Mao,Shih-En Wei*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: 提出了一种端到端的因果框架，通过动态多模态风格检索实现超低延迟、高保真的个性化音频驱动面部动画生成，无需音频前瞻或预编码静态嵌入。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有音频驱动面部动画框架无法兼顾实时流式传输与高保真个性化：要么依赖引入延迟的音频前瞻，要么需要高用户配合度预编码静态嵌入，无法捕捉动态个性特征。

Method: (1) 时间层次化运动表示：捕获全局时间上下文和高频细节，同时保持解码因果性；(2) 多模态风格检索器：联合查询音频和运动，动态提取风格先验而不破坏因果性。将两者集成到因果自回归架构中。

Result: 在唇形同步精度、身份一致性和感知真实感方面显著优于现有最先进方法，定量评估和用户研究均支持结论。

Conclusion: 动态多模态风格检索机制实现了模板数量和内容完全灵活的可扩展个性化，为实时流式场景下的高保真面部动画生成提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Audio-driven facial animation is essential for immersive digital interaction, yet existing frameworks fail to reconcile real-time streaming with high-fidelity personalization. Current methods often rely on latency-inducing audio look-ahead, or require high user compliance to pre-encode static embeddings that fails to capture dynamic idiosyncrasies. We present an end-to-end causal framework for personalizing causal facial motion generation via dynamic multi-modal style retrieval, enabling ultra-low latency while uniquely leveraging unstructured style references. We introduce two key innovations: (1) a temporal hierarchical motion representation that captures global temporal context and high-frequency details while maintaining decoding causality, and (2) a multi-modal style retriever that jointly queries audio and motion to dynamically extract stylistic priors without breaking causality. This mechanism allows for scalable personalization with total flexibility regarding the number and contents of templates. By integrating these components into a causal autoregressive architecture, our method significantly outperforms state-of-the-art approaches in lip-sync accuracy, identity consistency, and perceived realism, supported by extensive quantitative evaluations and user studies.

</details>


### [339] [Prox-E: Fine-Grained 3D Shape Editing via Primitive-Based Abstractions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23774)
*Etai Sella,Hao Phung,Nitay Amiel,Or Litany,Or Patashnik,Hadar Averbuch-Elor*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: Prox-E是一种无需训练的3D编辑框架，通过几何基元抽象和视觉语言模型实现细粒度、局部化的3D结构编辑，在保持物体整体身份的同时，比现有2D驱动3D编辑方法更有效地平衡身份保持、形状质量和指令保真度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于2D图像编辑模型的3D编辑流水线虽在外观修改上有效，但在需要局部结构变化并严格保持物体整体身份的细粒度3D编辑任务中存在局限。

Method: 首先将输入3D形状抽象为一组紧凑的几何基元；然后利用预训练的视觉语言模型(VLM)编辑该抽象表示，指定基元级别的变化；最后用这些结构编辑引导3D生成模型，实现细粒度局部修改的同时保留原始形状的未变化区域。

Result: 实验表明Prox-E在身份保持、形状质量和指令保真度三个指标上一致优于现有方法，包括基于2D的3D编辑器和基于训练的方法。

Conclusion: Prox-E通过显式的基元级几何抽象，在不需额外训练的情况下实现了更精细的3D结构控制，有效解决了2D驱动3D编辑中细粒度结构编辑的难题。

Abstract: Text-based 2D image editing models have recently reached an impressive level of maturity, motivating a growing body of work that heavily depends on these models to drive 3D edits. While effective for appearance-based modifications, such 2D-centric 3D editing pipelines often struggle with fine-grained 3D editing, where localized structural changes must be applied while strictly preserving an object's overall identity. To address this limitation, we propose Prox-E, a training-free framework that enables fine-grained 3D control through an explicit, primitive-based geometric abstraction. Our framework first abstracts an input 3D shape into a compact set of geometric primitives. A pretrained vision-language model (VLM) then edits this abstraction to specify primitive-level changes. These structural edits are subsequently used to guide a 3D generative model, enabling fine-grained, localized modifications while preserving unchanged regions of the original shape. Through extensive experiments, we demonstrate that our method consistently balances identity preservation, shape quality, and instruction fidelity more effectively than various existing approaches, including 2D-based 3D editors and training-based methods.

</details>


### [340] [MUSIC: Learning Muscle-Driven Dexterous Hand Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23886)
*Pei Xu,Yufei Ye,Shuchun Sun,Yu Ding,Elizabeth Schumann,C. Karen Liu*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: 本文提出一种数据驱动的物理仿真方法，通过分层强化学习架构（高频肌肉级控制+低频潜在空间协调）实现肌肉骨骼手精确弹奏钢琴，在未见过的乐谱上合成双手协调动作，达到最先进的物理驱动灵巧控制性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有灵巧手控制方法难以实现精细的双手协调动作（如钢琴演奏），且缺乏肌肉层面的生理合理性。本文旨在弥合高层动作规划与低层肌肉驱动之间的鸿沟，实现可泛化的、生理可信的灵巧控制。

Method: 分层架构：低层通过强化学习训练通用单手策略，追踪参考运动数据集生成肌肉-肌腱激活；将追踪策略蒸馏为VAE模型，获得平滑潜在空间；高层训练曲目专属策略，在潜在空间中根据乐谱音符事件协调双手运动。同时提出增强型肌肉骨骼手模型以支持精确手指控制。

Result: 在多种音乐风格的钢琴曲目上，该方法能合成精确按键的双手协调动作；在物理驱动灵巧控制中达到SOTA；肌肉骨骼手模型在生物力学稳定性和跟踪精度上优于现有模型；生成的激活模式与人类EMG记录一致。

Conclusion: 数据驱动的分层控制结合肌肉骨骼建模能有效实现生理可信的灵巧控制，且具备跨任务泛化能力；验证了该方法在精细动作合成和生物力学合理性方面的有效性。

Abstract: We present a data-driven approach for physics-based, muscle-driven dexterous control that enables musculoskeletal hands to perform precise piano playing for novel pieces of music outside the reference dataset. Our approach combines high-frequency muscle-level control with low-frequency latent-space coordination in a hierarchical architecture. At the low level, general single-hand policies are trained via reinforcement learning to generate dynamic muscle-tendon activations while tracking trajectories from a large reference motion dataset. The resulting tracking policies are then distilled into variational autoencoder (VAE) models, yielding smooth and structured latent spaces that abstract away low-level muscle dynamics. For the high level, we train piece-specific policies to operate in this latent space, coordinating bimanual motions based on specific goals, denoted by note events extracted from given musical scores, to synthesize performances beyond the reference data. In addition, we present an enhanced musculoskeletal hand model that supports fine control of fingers for accurate low-level motion tracking and diverse high-level motion synthesis. We evaluate the control pipeline of our approach on a diverse piano repertoire spanning multiple musical styles and technical demands. Results demonstrate that our approach can synthesize coordinated bimanual motions with accurate key presses, and achieve the state-of-the-art performance of piano playing in physics-based dexterous control. We also show that our musculoskeletal hand model demonstrates superior biomechanical stability and tracking precision compared to the existing model, and validate that our musculoskeletal hand model and muscle-driven controller can generate physiologically plausible activation patterns that align with human electromyography (EMG) recordings.

</details>


### [341] [Neural Enhancement of Analytical Appearance Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24081)
*Xuanzhe Shen,Xiaohe Ma,Kun Zhou,Hongzhi Wu*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: 本文提出神经增强框架，通过用小型多层感知器替换分析反射模型中的关键计算节点/算子，在保持紧凑性和可解释性的同时提升表达精度，实现准确、紧凑、高效且兼容标准渲染管线的混合反射模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统分析反射模型紧凑可解释但精度不足，神经模型拟合效果好但泛化性差且存储评估成本高。为结合两者优势并克服各自局限，提出神经增强框架。

Method: 在输入分析外观模型的计算图结构中，通过超立方体搜索自动高效识别待替换的节点/算子，将其替换为小型多层感知器（MLP），以可微分方式最大化增益，保留原模型计算图结构的同时提升表达能力。

Result: 增强后的BRDF模型同时具备准确性、紧凑性和高效性，在拟合实测反射率和双向纹理函数任务上优于现有最先进方法。

Conclusion: 神经增强框架有效融合分析与神经两类模型的优势，输出模型与标准光栅化或光线追踪管线完全兼容。

Abstract: Traditional analytical reflectance models, while compact and interpretable, lack the capacity to accurately represent physical measurements. Recent neural models, which closely fit input data, are less generalizable and often more expensive to store and evaluate. To combine the strengths and overcome the limitations of these two classes of models, we present neural enhancement, a novel framework to boost an input analytical appearance model, by identifying and replacing its key computational nodes/operators with small-scale multi-layer perceptrons. This allows us to leverage the computational graph structure of the original model, while improving its expressiveness at a modest cost. To make the enhancement computationally tractable, we propose a hypercube-based search to automatically and efficiently identify the node(s) and/or operator(s) to be replaced towards maximal gain in a differentiable fashion. We enhance a number of common analytical BRDF models. The results are, at once accurate, compact and efficient, and compare favorably with state-of-the-art work on fitting measured reflectance and bidirectional texture functions. Finally, our models are fully compatible with any standard rasterization or ray-tracing pipeline.

</details>


### [342] [Large-Scale Photogrammetric Documentation of St. John's Co-Cathedral: A Workflow for Cultural Heritage Preservation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24316)
*Matthew Kenely,Mark Bugeja,Andre Grima,Peter Pullicino,Matthew Pullicino,Dylan Seychell*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: 本文介绍了对马耳他瓦莱塔圣约翰联合大教堂（联合国教科文组织世界遗产）进行大规模摄影测量记录的综合方法。通过连续七个夜晚的数据采集，使用DSLR相机、无人机摄影和LiDAR扫描捕获了99,000张图像，创建了包含250-300亿个三角形的高细节3D重建模型。论文详细阐述了从多模态数据采集到处理的完整工作流程，包括应对复杂巴洛克建筑空间特有挑战（如高反射金属表面、深色材料、复杂挂毯和受限访问）的策略，并初步探索了高斯泼溅作为补充表示技术。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为文化遗产保护领域提供一种可大规模复制的摄影测量记录方法论，解决巴洛克风格建筑遗产数字化中面临的高反射表面、低光照、复杂几何结构等特殊挑战，生成高精度数字档案以支持灾难恢复、保护分析、虚拟旅游和学术研究。

Method: 采用多模态数据采集策略（DSLR、无人机、LiDAR）在夜间七天内采集99,000张图像；通过策略性图像分级和AI辅助去噪处理低光照颗粒噪声；进行大规模LiDAR点云清理；使用RealityCapture进行混合摄影测量重建；采用网格细分策略适配实时可视化引擎；结合自动化流程与必要的人工干预处理反射表面等复杂场景；初步实验高斯泼溅作为补充表示技术。

Result: 成功生成了包含250-300亿个三角形的超高细节3D重建模型，建立了可用于多种保护目的的完整数字档案，并提供了一套详细、可复制的工作流程。

Conclusion: 该工作为文化遗产专业人员提供了处理大规模建筑摄影测量记录项目的实用参考，有效解决了在复杂真实世界遗产场景中应用摄影测量方法的实际挑战。

Abstract: We present a comprehensive methodology for the large-scale photogrammetric documentation of St. John's Co-Cathedral in Valletta, Malta, a UNESCO World Heritage site renowned for its ornate Baroque architecture and Caravaggio masterpieces. Over seven nights of evening-only data collection, we captured 99,000 images using DSLR cameras, drone photography, and LIDAR scanning to create a highly detailed 3D reconstruction comprising 25-30 billion triangles. This paper documents our complete workflow for cultural heritage preservation, addressing the unique challenges of digitizing complex baroque architectural spaces with highly reflective metallic surfaces, dark materials, intricate tapestries, and restricted access. We detail our pipeline from multi-modal data acquisition through processing, including strategic image grading and AI-assisted denoising to address low-light grain, extensive LIDAR point cloud cleanup, hybrid photogrammetric reconstruction using RealityCapture, and mesh subdivision strategies for real-time visualization engines. Our methodology combines automated workflows with necessary manual intervention to handle the scale and complexity of the project, with particular attention to reflective surface challenges characteristic of baroque heritage sites. We also present preliminary experiments with Gaussian splatting as a complementary representation technique. The resulting digital archive serves multiple preservation purposes including disaster recovery documentation, conservation analysis, virtual tourism, and scholarly research. This work provides a detailed, replicable workflow for heritage professionals undertaking similar large-scale architectural documentation projects, addressing the practical challenges of applying photogrammetric methods in complex real-world heritage scenarios.

</details>

### [343] [Rejection Sampling is Optimal for Relative Entropy Coding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23076)
*Spencer Hill,Fady Alajaji,Tamás Linder,Gergely Flamich*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文构建了环投编码（ring toss code），证明了相对熵编码的速率下界为功能信息 $I_F(X \to Y)$，并实现了 $I_F(X \to Y) + \log e$ 比特的紧致上界，表明拒绝采样在相对熵编码中是最优的。该结果改进了经典互信息下界的可达间隙，并恢复了渐近二阶冗余结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 相对熵编码的经典结果表明互信息下界存在不可消除的对数间隙，说明互信息并非刻画其速率正确度量。Flamich等人（2025）提出了更紧的功能信息下界 $I_F(X \to Y)$，本文旨在证明该下界是紧的。

Method: 提出环投编码（ring toss code），一种针对拒绝采样的编码方法，利用功能信息 $I_F(X \to Y)$ 作为速率度量。

Result: 环投编码至多使用 $I_F(X \to Y) + \log e$ 比特；互信息下界在一般情况下可在 $\log(I(X;Y)+1)+2.45$ 比特内达到，奇异信道下为 $1.45$ 比特，均为目前最紧的界。

Conclusion: 拒绝采样是实现相对熵编码的最优方法，功能信息是比互信息更准确的速率度量，一-shot结果可恢复渐近二阶冗余结论。

Abstract: In relative entropy coding, a sender aims to design a stochastic code such that, on input $X \sim P_X$, the receiver can generate a sample $Y \sim P_{Y \mid X}$. It is a standard result that (1) this requires at least $I(X; Y)$ bits, (2) the lower bound is achievable within a logarithmic gap, and (3) this gap cannot be reduced in general. The necessity of the gap suggests that the mutual information is not the correct information measure to quantify the rate of relative entropy coding.
  A potential alternative emerged in the work of Flamich et al. (2025), who proved a tighter lower bound of $I_F(X \to Y)$, a quantity we call the functional information. In this paper, we show that this lower bound is tight by constructing the ring toss code, an encoding method for rejection sampling which uses at most $I_F(X \to Y) + \log e$ bits. This demonstrates that rejection sampling is optimal for relative entropy coding. Our result implies that the classical mutual information lower bound is achievable within $\log(I(X; Y) + 1) + 2.45$ bits in general and within $1.45$ bits for singular channels, which are both the tightest bounds of their kind to date. Moreover, our one-shot result also recovers Sriramu and Wagner's asymptotic results on the second-order redundancy of relative entropy codes.

</details>


### [344] [On the hull of linearized polynomial codes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23097)
*Daniele Bartoli,Giovanni Giuseppe Grimaldi,Pantelimon Stănică*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文利用统一的Gram矩阵方法，研究了由q-多项式算子定义的两类F_q-线性码的壳（hull）结构。对于图像码C(α)=im Φ_α，证明了壳维数与秩的关系式；对于F_{q^m}-线性秩距离码，推导了Gram矩阵决定壳维数，并在多种双射配置下给出了完整分类、LCD判据及密度渐近结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纠缠辅助量子纠错码中，壳（hull）的维度决定了所需预共享纠缠对的数量，因此研究线性码的壳结构对量子编码理论具有重要意义。本文旨在系统研究两类F_q-线性码的壳维数及其相关性质。

Method: 采用统一的Gram矩阵方法。对于图像码C(α)=im Φ_α，利用算子Φ_α及其关联Gram矩阵G(α)导出壳维数公式；对特定形式C_{λ,μ}=im(λx+μL(x))，得到二次Gram铅笔并利用判别式描述LCD轨迹。对于秩距离码，构造k×k Gram矩阵（含循环矩阵情形），通过迹-各向同性准则刻画极值条件。

Result: 1. 图像码壳维数公式：dim Hull(C(α)) = rank(Φ_α) - rank(G(α))；2. 二次Gram铅笔判别式描述LCD轨迹；3. 秩距离码中循环Gram矩阵的封闭形式判别式及三类双射配置的完整分类；4. 极值条件δ=d的显式迹-各向同性准则；5. LCD密度当q→∞时趋近于1；6. F_{64}上的计算实例及SageMath验证。

Conclusion: 本文建立了q-多项式算子码的壳维数统一框架，给出了LCD码的精确计数和密度渐近结果，为纠缠辅助量子纠错码的设计提供了理论基础和实用工具。

Abstract: Motivated by entanglement-assisted quantum error-correcting codes, where the hull dimension determines the number of required pre-shared entangled pairs, we study hulls of two families of $\mathbb{F}_q$-linear codes defined by $q$-polynomial operators over $\mathbb{F}_{q^m}$. Our main tool is a unified Gram-matrix method. For image codes $\mathcal{C}(\boldsymbolα)=\operatorname{im}Φ_{\boldsymbolα}$, with $Φ_{\boldsymbolα}=\sum_iα_iF_i$, we prove the master hull--rank formula $\dim\operatorname{Hull}(\mathcal{C}(\boldsymbolα))=\operatorname{rank}(Φ_{\boldsymbolα})-\operatorname{rank}(G(\boldsymbolα))$, where $G(\boldsymbolα)$ is the associated Gram matrix over $\mathbb{F}_q$. Specializing to $C_{λ,μ}=\operatorname{im}(λx+μL(x))$, we obtain a quadratic Gram pencil $λ^2G_0+λμG_1+μ^2G_2$ whose determinant describes the LCD locus in $\mathbb{P}^1(\mathbb{F}_q)$.
  We also treat $\mathbb{F}_{q^m}$-linear rank-distance codes $\mathcal{C}=\langle X,F_1,\ldots,F_k\rangle_{\mathbb{F}_{q^m}}$ with the Delsarte inner product, where a $k\times k$ Gram matrix over $\mathbb{F}_{q^m}$ determines the hull dimension. For $L(X)=X^{q^k}$, with $d=\gcd(k,m)$, the resulting circulant Gram matrices yield a closed-form discriminant and a complete classification in three of the four bijectivity configurations over $\mathbb{P}^1(\mathbb{F}_{q^m})$. In the remaining case, the hull dimension equals $δ=\dim_{\mathbb{F}_q}(\operatorname{im}φ_{λ,μ}\cap\kerφ_{λ,μ}^{\dagger})$, and the extremal condition $δ=d$ is characterized by an explicit trace-isotropy criterion. We conclude with an exact count of LCD and non-LCD points, showing that the LCD density tends to $1$ as $q\to\infty$, together with a worked example over $\mathbb{F}_{64}$ and a SageMath verification.

</details>

*Qingqing Peng,Dongxu Chang,Guiying Yan,Guanghui Wang*

TL;DR: 本文研究了在分层消息传递算法下，能够实现高效译码的广义低密度奇偶校验（GLDPC）码的调度序列特征，发现优先更新具有更大最小距离、更少最小重量码字和更短码长的子码对应的约束节点可提高译码效率，并据此设计了调度算法，通过仿真验证了其有效性。

Result: 仿真实验表明，所提出的调度算法能够有效提升GLDPC码的译码效率，验证了所总结的调度序列特征的有效性。

Abstract: In this study, we investigate the characteristics of scheduling sequences that enable efficient decoding of generalized low-density parity-check (GLDPC) codes under the layered message-passing algorithm. In particular, we show that scheduling sequences leading to higher decoding efficiency should prioritize the update of constraint nodes corresponding to subcodes with larger minimum distance, fewer minimum-weight codewords, and shorter code length. Based on these characteristics, we design a scheduling algorithm, which further demonstrates the effectiveness of these characteristics through simulation experiments.

### [346] [A Unified Fractional Regularization Framework for Sparse Recovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23184)

Method: 1) 提出 ℓ₁/ℓₚ^q 统一分数阶正则化框架；2) 刻画其一阶稳定点与 ℓ₁ - αℓₚ 模型的等价性；3) 基于 RIP 建立新的充分恢复条件；4) 开发 MM 算法并利用 KL 性质证明其收敛性。

Result: 所提出的分数阶正则化框架在不同感知矩阵和 MRI 重建任务中一致优于现有方法，在高相干感知矩阵下仍保持鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 本文成功构建了统一的分数阶正则化框架，从理论和算法两个层面为稀疏信号恢复提供了更优的解决方案，并为非凸正则化方法的统一理解奠定了理论基础。

Abstract: We propose a unified fractional regularization framework for sparse signal recovery based on the $\ell_1/\ell_p^q$ model. Our main theoretical contribution is the characterization of the equivalence between the first-order stationary points of the $\ell_1/\ell_p^q$ formulation and the subtractive $\ell_1 - α\ell_p$ model, providing a unified perspective on these nonconvex regularizers. In addition, we establish a new sufficient recovery condition under the Restricted Isometry Property (RIP), showing that the framework's robustness even under high-coherence sensing matrices. To solve the resulting problem, we develop a majorization-minimization (MM) algorithm and prove its convergence via the Kurdyka-Lojasiewicz (KL) property. Numerical experiments on different sensing matrices and MRI reconstruction demonstrate that the proposed approach consistently outperforms existing methods.

### [347] [Age of Information under Source-Aware Truncated ARQ in Multi-Source Wireless Status Updating](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23237)
*Tianci Zhang,Aobo Liu,Zhengchuan Chen,Zhong Tian,Jemin Lee,Yuquan Xiao,Mehul Motani*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种源感知截断ARQ（SATARQ）方案，通过差异化设置各源的最大传输次数来优化多源无线IoT状态更新系统的信息时效性。构建了多维年龄过程马尔可夫链模型，推导了AoI和峰值AoI的分布与平均值的解析表达式，分析了时效-能量权衡及能效，数值验证表明联合优化MTT、更新生成概率和传输功率可显著提升系统性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多源无线IoT状态更新系统中，不同信息源的重要性或更新频率存在差异，而传统ARQ协议对所有源采用相同的最大传输次数，无法实现差异化服务。本文旨在通过源感知的截断ARQ机制，在保证信息时效性的同时优化能量效率。

Method: 提出SATARQ方案，为不同源分配差异化的最大传输次数（MTT）；构建多维年龄过程（MDAP）马尔可夫链模型，同时追踪各源的AoI和当前传输更新的年龄；通过马尔可夫分析推导AoI与峰值AoI的分布和平均值，以及平均功耗的解析表达式。

Result: 获得了AoI和峰值AoI的分布与平均值的解析表达式；揭示了MTT、更新生成概率和传输功率对时效-能量权衡的影响；数值结果验证了理论分析的准确性；联合优化MTT、UGP和TP可显著改善多源系统的整体时效-能量权衡和能效。

Conclusion: SATARQ方案结合MTT、UGP和TP的联合优化，能够有效改善多源无线IoT状态更新系统的信息时效性与能量效率之间的权衡关系，优于传统统一截断ARQ方案。

Abstract: This paper studies information timeliness in multi-source wireless Internet of Things (IoT) status updating systems under a truncated Automatic Repeat reQuest (ARQ) protocol. We propose a source-aware truncated ARQ (SATARQ) scheme that allows differentiated maximum transmission times (MTTs) tailored to different sources. This work focuses on a wireless system with preemptive update management. To study the statistical characteristics of the age of information (AoI) process for each source, a multi-dimensional age process (MDAP) is developed and modeled as a Markov chain, tracking both the AoI and the age of the concerned source's update currently in transmission. Via Markov analysis of the MDAP, we obtain analytical expressions for the distributions and averages of the AoI and peak AoI, as well as the average power consumption of IoT device. The timeliness-energy tradeoff is analyzed by examining the impact of the MTT, update generation probability (UGP), and wireless transmission power (TP). Moreover, this work explores the energy efficiency of the wireless status updating process and its relationship with the information timeliness and energy cost. Numerical results validate the theoretical analysis. Finally, it is demonstrated that the proposed SATARQ, combined with the optimization of MTTs, UGPs, and TPs, significantly improves the overall timeliness-energy tradeoff and energy efficiency across all sources.

### [348] [On the Minimum Distances of Some Families of BCH Codes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23594)
*Yaqi Chen,Hao Chen,Cunsheng Ding,Huimin Lao*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文通过显式构造最小重量码字的定位多项式，解决了多类无限族窄感BCH码的最小距离问题，证明了在多种参数条件下最小距离等于设计距离，并部分证实了Ding等人提出的猜想。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: BCH码的最小距离确定是一个极具挑战性的问题，已有的BCH界仅提供下界，精确的最小距离难以获知。本文旨在通过构造定位多项式，确定多类无限族窄感BCH码的真实最小距离。

Method: 通过显式构造最小重量码字的定位多项式，分别处理本原BCH码和非本原BCH码。对于本原BCH码，构造了在$\mathbb{F}_3$和$\mathbb{F}_4$上设计距离$\delta\in\{5,6,7,8\}$的无限族以及$2\le\delta\le q-1$的$q$元无限族；对于$\delta=q^t+1$的情形，利用模$pt$同余条件证明了最小距离等于设计距离。对于非本原BCH码，构造了参数满足特定条件的族。

Result: 1) 得到$\mathbb{F}_3$和$\mathbb{F}_4$上设计距离$\delta\in\{5,6,7,8\}$的无限族本原BCH码满足$d=\delta$；2) 得到$2\le\delta\le q-1$的$q$元BCH码无限族满足$d=\delta$；3) 证明当$m\equiv0\pmod{pt}$时，码$\mathbf{C}_{(q,q^m-1,q^t+1,1)}$的最小距离$d=\delta=q^t+1$，部分证实了Ding等人的猜想；4) 构造了非本原BCH码无限族满足$d=\delta=p+1$。

Conclusion: 本文系统性地解决了多类无限族BCH码的最小距离确定问题，部分证实了已有猜想，为BCH码最小距离的理论分析提供了新的构造方法和重要结果。

Abstract: BCH codes form an important class of cyclic codes, which have applications in communication and data storage systems. Although the BCH bound provides a lower bound on the minimum distance of BCH codes, determining the true minimum distances of BCH codes is a very challenging problem. In this paper, we settle the minimum distances of a number of infinite families of narrow-sense BCH codes.
  By explicitly constructing the locator polynomials for minimum weight codewords, we obtain many families of primitive and non-primitive BCH codes with $d=δ$, where $d$ is the minimum distance of a $q$-ary BCH code of length $n$, designed distance $δ$, and offset $b$, denoted by $\mathbf{C}_{(q, n, δ, b)}$. For primitive BCH codes, we obtain infinite families of BCH codes over $\mathbb{F}_3$ and $\mathbb{F}_4$ satisfying $d=δ$, where $δ\in \{5,6,7,8\}$. Moreover, we construct several infinite families of $q$-ary BCH codes with $d=δ$, where $2 \le δ\le q-1$. For $δ=q^t+1$, we prove that the BCH code $\mathbf{C}_{(q, q^m-1, q^t+1, 1)}$ has $d=δ$ for all $m$ satisfying $m \equiv 0 \pmod{pt}$, where $p$ denotes the characteristic of $\mathbb{F}_q$. In the paper by Ding et al., IEEE Trans. Inf. Theory 61(5): 2351-2356, it was conjectured that the minimum distance of $\mathbf{C}_{(q, q^m-1, q^t+1, 1)}$ is always equal to its Bose distance $d_B$. Our result confirms this conjecture for the case $m \equiv 0 \pmod{pt}$. For non-primitive BCH codes, we construct a family of BCH codes $\mathbf{C}_{(q,\frac{q^p-1}λ,p+1,1)}$ with $d=δ=p+1$, where $p$ is an odd prime, $q=p^e$ with $p \nmid e$ and $λ\mid q-1$.

</details>

### [350] [Sensing-Assisted Secure Communication in MA-Aided ISAC: CRB Analysis and Robust Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23663)
*Yaxuan Chen,Guangchi Zhang,Miao Cui,Hao Fu,Qingqing Wu,Rui Zhang*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文针对物理层安全中窃听者信道状态信息难以获取的挑战，利用通感一体化系统的感知能力，提出了一种面向移动天线辅助ISAC系统的感知辅助安全通信方案。该方案通过两阶段设计（窃听者离开角感知与安全通信），联合优化移动天线的位置和鲁棒波束成形，以提升感知精度并最大化保密速率，仿真验证了其显著优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 物理层安全的核心挑战在于难以获取潜在窃听者的信道状态信息，而通感一体化系统的固有感知功能为估计窃听者关键参数（如离开角）提供了有前景的解决方案。

Method: 提出两阶段方案：第一阶段，基站优化发射和接收移动天线的位置以提升感知精度，推导了估计离开角的闭式克拉美-罗界；第二阶段，通过设计考虑离开角不确定区域的鲁棒波束成形向量并优化发射移动天线位置来最大化保密速率。将非凸联合优化问题分解为两个子问题：采用交替优化算法求解CRB最小化问题；采用反向归纳法、凸包构造和交替优化相结合的方法求解最坏情况保密速率最大化问题。

Result: 仿真结果表明所提方案相较于多种基准方案具有显著优势。

Conclusion: 通过移动天线位置优化与鲁棒波束成形的联合设计，能够有效提升ISAC系统在窃听者CSI未知场景下的安全通信性能。

Abstract: A core challenge in physical-layer security is the difficulty of obtaining the channel state information (CSI) of potential eavesdroppers. The inherent sensing functionality of integrated sensing and communication (ISAC) systems offers a promising solution by enabling the estimation of key parameters, such as the eavesdropper's angles of departure (AoDs). Capitalizing on this capability, we propose a sensing-assisted secure communication scheme for a movable antenna (MA)-aided ISAC system. The scheme comprises two stages: eavesdropper AoD sensing and secure communication. In the first stage, the base station (BS) optimizes the positions of its transmit and receive MAs to enhance sensing accuracy. We derive the closed-form Cramer-Rao bound (CRB) for the estimated AoDs to fundamentally characterize how MA positions influence the estimation uncertainty. In the second stage, the BS ensures secure communication by designing a robust beamforming vector that accounts for the AoD uncertainty region and by further optimizing the transmit MAs' positions to maximize the secrecy rate. To manage the end-to-end design, we formulate a joint optimization problem. This intractable non-convex problem is decomposed into two subproblems. For the first subproblem, we develop an alternating optimization (AO) algorithm to solve the CRB minimization problem. For the second subproblem, we solve the worst-case secrecy rate maximization problem using a method based on backward induction, convex hull construction, and AO. Finally, simulation results are provided to demonstrate the significant advantages of the proposed scheme compared to various benchmarks.

</details>


### [351] [Sub-Nyquist Sampling for Reaching Theoretical Minimal Sampling Rate Boundary](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24434)
*Dong Xiao,Jian Wang*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种双频率混叠宽带转换器（DAWC），能在未知子带位置的情况下以理论最低采样率实现完美的子带定位和波形重建，并设计了基于边信息辅助的子空间追踪算法（MSSP）来精确恢复频谱支撑集，在噪声环境下具有稳定恢复保证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有亚奈奎斯特采样方案在盲场景（子带位置未知）下所需采样率至少为理论最小值的两倍，因此需要一种能在未知子带位置条件下达到理论最低采样率的宽带频谱感知方案。

Method: 提出DAWC架构，将多频带频谱划分为非均匀频率区间并选择性采样子集；设计MSSP算法，利用信号列子矩阵中固有的公共支撑结构进行频谱支撑集精确恢复；基于RIP给出噪声环境下的稳定恢复保证。

Result: 在信号和系统的温和条件下，DAWC能以理论最低采样率实现完美的子带定位和波形重建；数值仿真表明，所提方案在频谱恢复精度上优于现有方法。

Conclusion: DAWC结合MSSP算法可在盲场景下达到理论最低采样率，实现高精度宽带频谱感知，且具有噪声鲁棒性。

Abstract: Wideband spectrum sensing motivates sub-Nyquist sampling architectures that exploit spectral sparsity, yet in blind scenarios where subband locations are unknown, existing schemes require sampling rates at least twice the theoretical minimum. To this end, we propose a dual-frequency aliasing wideband converter (DAWC), which partitions the multiband spectrum into non-uniform frequency intervals and selectively samples only a subset of them, requiring no prior knowledge of subband locations. We demonstrate that under mild conditions on the signal and the system, DAWC achieves perfect subband localization and waveform reconstruction at the theoretical minimum rate. Moreover, we introduce an innovative side-information-aided subspace pursuit (MSSP) algorithm exploiting the common support structure inherent in the signal column submatrices for exact recovery of the spectrum support set. Based on the restricted isometry property (RIP), we provide stable recovery guarantees for MSSP in the presence of noise. Numerical simulations show that the proposed scheme achieves superior spectrum recovery accuracy compared to state-of-the-art methods.
