### [352] [Fisher Information and Dynamical Sampling I](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24499)
*Mattia Carrino,Stefan Hohenegger*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究了从时间序列测量数据重建动力系统时，Fisher信息的偏差问题。证明了自由度聚类可以减少偏差、提高重建精度，并提供了量化信息损失的方法，通过简单区室模型验证了结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在实际应用中，我们无法直接获取动力系统的连续曲线C，只能从有限样本的时间序列测量数据中重建系统。因此需要定量评估从采样数据中重建动力系统Fisher信息的准确性，即计算Fisher信息在大样本下的偏差。

Method: 推导了Fisher信息在大样本n下的偏差表达式；基于此结果证明自由度聚类能降低偏差；结合近期提出的聚类方案，量化评估信息损失；通过流行病学启发的简单区室模型进行数值验证。

Result: 自由度的聚类可以降低Fisher信息的偏差，从而提高从给定采样数据中描述新系统的准确性；提供了量化信息损失的评估方法，能估计从有限数据中可靠提取系统动力学信息的程度。

Conclusion: 该工作的结果适用于具有多自由度的广义动力学模型，而不仅限于流行病学场景，为从采样数据中准确重建系统动力学提供了理论指导。

Abstract: Information theory is a powerful framework to capture aspects of dynamical systems with multiple degrees of freedom. Mathematically, the dynamics can be represented as a continuous curve $\mathcal{C}$ on a suitable hyperplane in flat space and the Fisher information provides the norm of an infinitesimal displacement along this curve. In many applications, however, we do not have direct access to $\mathcal{C}$. Instead, we have to reconstruct the latter from a time-series of measurements (obtained as samples of size $n$), which are represented by an ordered set of points $\widehat{\mathcal{C}}$ on the same hyperplane. In this work, we calculate the bias of the Fisher information for large $n$, which provides a quantitative estimation for how accurately the dynamics of a system can be reconstructed from a given set of sampled data. Based on this result, we show that a clustering of the degrees of freedom reduces the bias and thus improves the accuracy with which the new system can be described with the same data. Inspired by a recent proposal for such a clustering, we provide a quantitive assessment of the loss of information, which allows to estimate how much information about the dynamics of a system can reliably be extracted based on a given set of data. We illustrate our findings in the case of a simple compartmental model. Although the latter is inspired by epidemiology, the results of this work are applicable to very general dynamical models with multiple degrees of freedom.

</details>


### [353] [Densification Converses for Walker Constellations With Explicit Constants and Reuse Scaling Laws](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24656)
*Ali Khalesi,François Baccelli*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文证明Walker LEO星座在全频率复用、最近可视关联下，随着卫星总数N→∞，下行SINR覆盖概率和遍历频谱效率均以O(1/N)速率趋零，出现“致密化崩溃”；避免崩溃需频率复用因子Ω(N)或活动概率q满足qN=O(1)。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示Walker LEO星座在密集化部署下性能退化的根本机制，尤其是地球几何约束（可视帽）导致的干扰线性增长与有用信号有界之间的失衡，为星座规模设计提供理论边界。

Method: 基于Walker星座/地球动力学的不变（平稳）测度建立相态模型；提出确定性可视环空引理，证明固定比例可视卫星位于地平线内严格距离环空中；利用功率律路径损耗、两级天线增益模型、i.i.d.衰落（单位均值有限二阶矩）和非零噪声推导非渐近上界。

Result: 总干扰至少线性增长于N，有用信号一致有界；覆盖概率和遍历频谱效率均以O(1/N)上界趋零；频率复用（独立稀疏化）下需qN=O(1)才可避免崩溃，对应O(1/(qN))上界。

Conclusion: Walker LEO星座在全频率复用下必然遭遇致密化崩溃，必须通过线性比例的频率复用或等效的稀疏化来维持性能，揭示星座密集化部署的根本性权衡。

Abstract: We establish densification converses for Walker LEO constellations under nearest-visible association in the full-frequency-reuse setting. Performance is evaluated under the invariant (stationary) measure induced by the constellation/Earth dynamics on the user--constellation ``phase state.'' A key Walker-specific feature, absent from unbounded planar models, is that association is restricted to a bounded visible cap determined by Earth geometry. Under power-law path-loss, a two-level antenna-gain model, i.i.d.\ nonnegative fading with unit mean and finite second moment, and nonzero noise, we prove that increasing the total satellite count $N=N_oN_s$ forces the aggregate interference to grow at least linearly in $N$, while the useful signal remains uniformly bounded above. Consequently, the downlink SINR coverage probability at any fixed threshold and the ergodic spectral efficiency both vanish as $N\to\infty$. The key technical ingredient is a deterministic visibility-annulus block lemma, uniform over all sufficiently large constellations and all "phase states", showing that a fixed fraction of visible satellites lies in a distance annulus strictly inside the horizon; this yields explicit finite-$N$ collapse bounds. In particular, we derive nonasymptotic $O(1/N)$ upper bounds on both coverage and ergodic spectral efficiency. Finally, in the case of frequency reuse through independent thinning, with activity probability $q$, we show that avoiding densification collapse necessarily requires $qN=O(1)$, equivalently a reuse factor $Ω(N)$, and we obtain a corresponding explicit $O(1/(qN))$ upper bound.

</details>

### [354] [Strategically Robust Aggregative Games](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23669)
*Andreas Feik,Nicolas Lanzetti,Saverio Bolognani,Florian Dörfler,Dario Paccagnan*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为“策略鲁棒Wardrop均衡”的新均衡概念，通过最优传输模糊集保护智能体免受群体聚合行为偏差的影响，可在标准Wardrop均衡（无鲁棒性）与安全策略（最大鲁棒性）之间插值，并在凸聚合博弈中证明了纯策略均衡的存在性与可计算性。在电动车充电案例中，该均衡不仅保护智能体免受不确定性影响，还发现了“通过鲁棒化实现协调”效应，降低了所有智能体的均衡成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多智能体决策场景（如电动车充电、交通路径规划）中，智能体面临他人行为的多源不确定性（信息不完备、计算受限、有限理性），这些不确定性最终影响群体聚合行为。现有方法难以显式建模所有不确定性来源，因此需要一种直接针对群体聚合行为偏差提供保护的新框架。

Method: 基于策略鲁棒博弈论，每个智能体针对以群体聚合行为为中心的最优传输模糊集内的最坏情况聚合行为进行自我保护。由此定义策略鲁棒Wardrop均衡，可在无鲁棒性（标准Wardrop均衡）与最大鲁棒性（安全策略）之间平滑插值。在凸聚合博弈设定下证明纯策略均衡的存在性，并提供可计算的求解工具。

Result: 在凸聚合博弈中证明了纯策略鲁棒Wardrop均衡的存在性，并给出了可计算的方法。电动车充电应用表明，该均衡能帮助智能体做出更优决策，保护其免受群体聚合行为不确定性的影响。还发现了“协调-鲁棒化”效应：策略鲁棒性反而降低了所有智能体的均衡成本。

Conclusion: 策略鲁棒Wardrop均衡为多智能体系统中的不确定聚合行为提供了一种灵活且可计算的鲁棒决策框架，不仅提供了保护，还可能通过鲁棒化意外地促进协调，降低整体成本。

Abstract: In many multiagent settings, such as electric vehicle charging and traffic routing, agents must make decisions in the face of uncertain behavior exhibited by others. Often, this uncertainty arises from multiple sources, such as incomplete information, limited computation, or bounded rationality, ultimately impacting the aggregate behavior. To tackle this challenge, we follow recent work on strategically robust game theory and postulate that agents seek protection directly against deviations around the emergent behavior, as opposed to explicitly modeling all sources of uncertainty. Specifically, we propose that each agent protects itself against the worst-case aggregate behavior within an optimal-transport-based ambiguity set centered at the emergent aggregate population behavior. This leads to a novel equilibrium concept, called strategically robust Wardrop equilibrium, that enables one to interpolate between standard Wardrop equilibria (no robustness) and security strategies (maximum robustness). In the setting of convex aggregative games, we establish the existence of a pure strategically robust Wardrop equilibrium and provide tractable computational tools for computing it. Through an application in electric vehicle charging, we demonstrate that strategically robust Wardrop equilibria lead to better decisions, protecting agents against the uncertain aggregate behavior of the population. Remarkably, we also observe that strategic robustness can lead to lower equilibrium costs for all agents, uncovering a "coordination-via-robustification" effect.

</details>


### [355] [Learning is Revelation in Disguise: Improved Regret and Equivalence Results for Dynamic Pricing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24093)
*Shiliang Zuo*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文研究动态定价中卖家与战略性非短视买家的交互，证明了菜单机制能实现更优的遗憾界，并建立了间接学习机制与直接显示机制在最优遗憾上的等价性，揭示学习即揭示的本质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动态定价问题处于自适应学习与机制设计的交叉点，但两者关系尚不明确。现有工作仅关注标价机制，忽视了更丰富的机制设计空间，且学习范式与揭示范式之间的理论联系缺失。

Method: 通过理论分析，首先证明菜单机制（提供分配-支付合约）能够实现 $O(T_γ\log T_γ)$ 的遗憾界，其中 $T_γ$ 是买家的有效贴现时间水平；其次建立间接学习机制与直接显示机制之间的最优遗憾等价关系。

Result: 菜单机制显著改进了所有现有遗憾界；间接学习机制与直接显示机制的最优遗憾完全相同，即学习范式与揭示范式等价。

Conclusion: 在线学习的自适应数据驱动算法与显式类型揭示是解决同一问题的两种语言，学习本质上是揭示的一种形式，两者在最优遗憾意义上等价。

Abstract: We study dynamic pricing where a seller repeatedly interacts with a strategic, non-myopic buyer who has a fixed private valuation and discounts future utility. Prior work focused exclusively on posted-price mechanisms, which only extract binary accept/reject signals. For our first result, we show that menu mechanisms-offering allocation-payment contracts are able to achieve $O(T_γ\log T_γ)$ regret, where $T_γ$ is the buyer's effective discounted time horizon, improving all prior bounds. Our second contribution is more conceptual in nature. The problem of dynamic pricing sits at the intersection of two paradigms: adaptive learning in computer science / machine learning and revelation-principle-based mechanism design in economics-yet their relationship has remained unclear. We establish a fundamental equivalence: indirect learning mechanisms and direct revelation mechanisms achieve identical optimal regret. The adaptive, data-driven algorithms of online learning and explicit type elicitation are two languages towards solving the same problem; hence, learning is revelation in disguise.

### [356] [Explanation Systems for Approval-Based Multiwinner Voting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24307)
*Niclas Boehmer,Luca Kreisel,Jannik Peters*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文提出基于价格系统（price system）的框架，用于量化分析批准制多赢家投票中委员会对选民的代表性，包括选民影响力分配、候选人支持来源等解释机制，并进行了公理化研究与算法设计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究主要关注二元比例公理（判断委员会是否比例代表），但缺乏细粒度量化描述委员会如何代表选民、选民影响力如何分配、候选人为何入选或落选等解释性信息。

Method: 基于priceability概念提出价格系统框架：每位选民有预算，用于购买其认可的当选候选人（单位价格）。对价格系统提出多条公理（结构一致性、影响力归因、比例对齐），并设计多项式时间算法（选民持续获得并行使影响力），在合成与真实数据上进行实验验证。

Result: 提出的计算规则满足所有可联合满足的公理；实验表明该解释体系与已有比例性概念相关，并能有效检测存在的不平等影响力。

Abstract: In approval-based multiwinner voting, voters express approval preferences over a set of candidates, and the goal is to return a winning committee. This model captures a broad range of subset selection problems under preferences. Prior work has focused on the study of binary proportionality axioms that certify whether a given committee is proportionally representative or not. We take a more fine-grained perspective and initiate the study of explanation systems that quantify how a committee represents the electorate, i.e., how much influence each voter exerts, how this influence is allocated across selected candidates, how each candidate is backed by the voters, and why certain candidates were not chosen.
  Building on the notion of priceability, we propose price systems as a framework for such explanations. A price system assigns each voter an individual budget, which they can spend on selected candidates they approve, and each candidate needs to be purchased at a unit price. Since many price systems can exist for a given outcome, selecting among them requires care. We initiate an axiomatic study of price systems and propose several axioms capturing structural coherence, faithful attribution of influence, and alignment with proportionality. On the algorithmic side, we introduce a polynomial-time computable rule in which voters continuously gain and exercise influence and show that it satisfies all jointly satisfiable axioms. Experiments on synthetic and real-world instances indicate that our explanations correlate with established proportionality notions and can recover unequal influence when it is present.

### [357] [Private Private Information in Second-Price Auction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24530)
*Boyu Liu,Wei Tang,Zihe Wang,Shuo Zhang*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文研究在第二价格拍卖中，当卖方承诺采用"私有的私有信息结构"（即竞拍者的信号事先独立，但竞拍者对估值共享一个对称且任意相关的先验分布）时，信息的独立性问题。结果显示：虽可通过私有私有信息结构实现最优效率与完全剩余提取，但该均衡可能不稳定；进一步可构造严格均衡以接近最大福利；同时证明了无法精确实现最大福利的不可行性，并给出了充要条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典结果表明，即使竞拍者信息之间存在任意小的相关性，也能在拍卖中实现完全剩余提取。这种"脆弱性"促使作者研究当卖方承诺信息独立（信号事前独立）时，信息结构对剩余提取和效率的影响。

Method: 文章在第二价格拍卖框架下，定义"私有的私有信息结构"（信号独立但估值先验相关），首先证明存在性，然后构造严格均衡，最后给出可达福利/收益对的完全刻画。

Result: (1) 私有私有信息结构总能实现最优效率和完全剩余提取，但均衡可能不稳定；(2) 可构造严格均衡使收益任意接近最大福利；(3) 一般情况下无法精确实现最大福利，并给出了充要条件；(4) 对一般信息结构给出了可达（竞拍者剩余，卖方收益）对的完整刻画。

Conclusion: 信息独立性在拍卖设计中具有微妙的限制：虽然可以逼近最优结果，但精确实现存在障碍，且均衡稳定性是关键约束。

Abstract: Classic results show that even an arbitrarily small correlation across bidders' information can enable full surplus extraction in auctions and related mechanism design settings. Motivated by this fragility, we study the information independence in a second-price auction when the seller commits to a private private information structure, meaning bidders' signals are independent ex ante, while bidders share a symmetric and arbitrarily correlated prior distribution over their valuations. We first show that the seller optimal efficient outcome with full surplus extraction can always be implemented by a private private information structure that admits a Bayes Nash equilibrium. However, this equilibrium may not be stable. We then further construct a private private information structure that achieves revenue arbitrarily close to maximum welfare while admitting a strict equilibrium. At the same time, we establish an impossibility result: under private private information, in general, bidder surplus cannot achieve maximal welfare exactly, and we characterize necessary and sufficient conditions on the prior distribution under which bidder surplus can be made arbitrarily close to maximal welfare. We then explore which other efficient outcomes are achievable under private private information. Finally, moving beyond private private information, we provide a complete characterization of the achievable pairs (bidder surplus, seller revenue) under general information structures.

</details>
